  • Chapter 1157: Fishing!

In the Fifth Star Ring, near the border separating the south and the west, the crimson aurora shone above as sticky rain fell in all directions. A great wind blew, removing even more moisture from the rain, turning it into a glue that had immense sealing power. In fact, in some areas on the fringe, it had turned into a solid gel.

Not even the air could escape the effects. It was as if the space in this entire area was being solidified by the glue. It was astonishingly mighty and terrifyingly deadly.

Xu Qing was right in the middle of it all. He was covered in the sticky rain, which formed fluidic strands connecting him to the land, the air, and everything else in the area. It was completely stuck even to his skin.

Everything was rapidly turning into a thick gel, and the effects were only speeding up. If he couldn’t free himself soon, and the wind dried everything up, he would be like an object encased in amber. Escape would be completely impossible.

But Xu Qing didn’t seem anxious. He had a way to deal with this glue magic. Because of that, he was focused on analyzing, not the fighting, but rather, factors beyond the field of battle, including the inner state of the young man that was his opponent. Although such things might seem like they weren’t relevant to the actual fighting, the reality was that they were key to everything.

Normally speaking, this person shouldn’t be going for broke this early in the Trial of the Hunt. After all, the second round had just started, and fighting like this right now wouldn’t be worth it. If you ended up seriously injured, then you would be in great danger. Later on, there would surely be even more dangerous situations to deal with.

What was more, Xu Qing only had a total of two medallions, which wouldn’t be worth the effort this young man was putting forth. Given this person’s battle prowess, there had to be other targets that would be easier to deal with. Risking one’s life in such a silly way wasn’t something an intelligent person would do.

There’s definitely something fishy going on.

With such thoughts going through his head, Xu Qing looked at the distant horizon. Everything seemed to be confirming his speculations. A feeling of determination grew within him. As the wind blew and the glue hardened, the sealing effects were locking down everything in the area.

I can’t worry too much about the details. Even if I get injured in the process, I need to end this fight quickly.

Eyes flashing with a mysterious light, he exercised a thought, and the blood in his body suddenly started racing much more quickly through him. A tremor passed through him as he shockingly forced all of his blood out through his pores.

It poured out without cease, turning into a blood mist that surrounded him. The blood spread, providing moisture to heaven and earth.

This was a technique he had picked up from the city magistrate he killed earlier. He drew out his own blood, infused it with his will, and sent it out to slow down the hardening effect caused by the wind.

As a result, the moisture the rain had lost was returned. At the same time, the sticky rain turned crimson. What was more, the wind couldn’t blow as freely.

This magic that turned rain into glue was definitely unusual, and shockingly mighty, but it had a weakness. Specifically, the stickiness could only be unleashed when the wind dried it out.

The young man was obviously aware of that weakness, which was why he rarely used this technique in direct attacks. Normally speaking, he would unleash it from a hiding spot to catch someone off guard, and then swoop in to kill them before they recovered. What was more, he wasn’t using it right now in the hopes of killing his opponent. He was just trying to buy time.

When he realized that Xu Qing had already identified the weakness of the technique, the young man scowled. That said, he wasn’t very surprised. He had realized much earlier that this enemy was very intelligent and reacted quickly. He was definitely a formidable opponent. He hadn’t really intended for his glue magic to simply seal this person.

Though he regretted that his opponent reacted so quickly, he didn’t hesitate to fall back and simultaneously performed a double-handed incantation gesture. Without a second thought, he drew deeply on his cultivation base to bolster his wind authority to try to counter what Xu Qing was doing.

One was using the wind to dry things out, the other was adding the moisture back. As long as one could identify the most salient aspect of the situation, it was possible to force a state of balance....

Though the young man hadn’t completely succeeded at sealing the area, he had at least slowed down his opponent and bought some time.

Besides, the glue covering his opponent, though it had been prevented from hardening by the moisture in the blood mist, was still sticky. The limitations it enforced were continuing.

The young man’s reactions went to show how skilled and talented he was. He was really top-notch. After all, it was completely proper to say that his strategy was working exactly as intended.

What was more, his technique also accounted for Xu Qing’s Fishing the Moon in the Well, although he had bypassed that necessity by starting out with his five-colored painting, which drained Xu Qing’s spatial magic. He was fully aware that spatial magics like those used by Xu Qing could most likely be used multiple times in a row. And either way, draining his opponent was the best thing to do. Using his glue on everything in the area, even the space, would also do a lot to prevent his opponent from using his spatial magics.

If he finds another weakness, then I don’t think I can keep fighting. Besides, I already sent the location information to the relevant party. If he takes too long to get here, that’s not my fault.

With such thoughts on his mind, the young man bolstered the wind again, all while sending out his authority of fire. Simultaneously, he backed up and started getting ready with his next move.

Unfortunately... something happened then that was not only incredibly shocking, but also, was something he hadn’t predicted. The countless strands of glue connected to Xu Qing suddenly started whipping back and forth and emanating a heaven-shaking, earth-shattering sword energy.

That sword energy... came from The Emperor’s Sword. The energy wasn’t severing the strands of glue. Thanks to the young man continuously bolstering his own magic, The Emperor’s Sword actually couldn’t do that.

Instead, the might of the sword was building up inside of Xu Qing.

He was severing... his own skin!

In the blink of an eye, the incisive power of The Emperor’s Sword savagely sliced back and forth within his own skin. It was separating his own muscles from his skin!

A blinding sword nimbus erupted around him. In the blink of an eye, Xu Qing’s body was seemingly split into two parts. A gaping wound opened up, starting at the top of his head, slicing down through his face, chest, and the rest of his body....

His skin was being opened like a garment. Astonishingly, a skinless figure made only of bloody flesh shot out into the open. It moved at top speed. Before any of the strands of glue could latch onto it, it took advantage of its freedom to unleash a spatial manipulation magic.

An instant later, Xu Qing had teleported away.

The young man with the birthmark watched this happen, and his pupils constricted rapidly, and his heart started pounding with alarm. He had encountered vicious people before, but never before had he seen this level of ferocity. This person abandoned his own skin to escape!

The young man shot back at top speed, an intense sensation of deadly crisis filling him. He knew that his opponent definitely wasn’t paying this extremely heavy price just to make an escape. Sadly for him, his realization, and his fast retreat, were both too slow.

The moment Xu Qing was free, he unleashed his dao of space. A grid appeared, spreading out in layers and turning into a sealing power that crushed down onto the young man. An ancient sundial also manifested behind Xu Qing, its gnomon spinning as his dao of time appeared. This was the power to freeze time!

He used space to cut off the path of retreat. He used time to subdue the timescape.

As a result, the young man lurched to a halt in midair. His body stopped moving. His soul stopped moving. Space was locked down. Time was frozen.

And then... the sword energy came out.

This was the second of the five streams of sword energy that Grandpa Ninth had given to Xu Qing. When it exploded out, wild colors flashed in heaven and earth. Winds screamed.

Sword energy slashed toward the young man. This young man was an extraordinary opponent. It was a moment of crisis, and despite the fact that both space and time had been locked down, he still was able to react. An aura of self-detonation suddenly built up around him. He was going to use the might of self-detonation to shake space and time, and hopefully free himself.

Xu Qing’s spatial grid trembled. Cracks spread out across it. The sundial behind him shook violently and also started to crack.

It was about to explode.

After all... this opponent was very close to being a mid Imperial Sovereign, and had developed his authorities almost to their limit.

At that critical moment, Xu Qing’s eyes flashed with cold light. Despite the spatial vibrations and the cracks spreading out on the sundial, Xu Qing just focused on unleashing the sword energy. Sword energy swept forth. Light filled heaven and earth, and a thunderous rumbling drifted out.

Then, there was a bang... as the sword energy landed on the young man’s forehead, pierced into his body, and destroyed everything it touched! He was killed in body and soul! All of this takes a bit of time to describe, but actually happened in the time it takes a spark to fly off a piece of flint.

In the blink of an eye, the range of Xu Qing’s permission medallion was increased, reaching a level of 5,000,000.

However, he had no time to study what was within range, as he suddenly coughed up a huge mouthful of blood. His flesh was completely mangled; the injuries he had suffered were not insignificant.

What had been difficult about this fight wasn’t the actual fighting techniques, but rather, ending it quickly. Despite his use of both space and time, his opponent had very nearly slipped free. It was easy to imagine what would have happened if he didn’t have the level of control he did over space and time. Even his sudden use of that sword energy might not have been successful.

And if he had failed, then after his opponent got free, it was entirely possible he would have started fighting again.

Xu Qing took a deep breath. Right now, he didn’t have time to focus on healing up. He quickly took stock of the battlefield, all while suppressing the pain he felt from losing his skin, as well as the backlash from using his space and time abilities. He burst into motion.

This fight shouldn’t have been so desperate.

As he sped along, Xu Qing thought regretfully about how things had played out. If his opponent hadn’t been acting so suspiciously, Xu Qing wouldn’t have been forced to pay this price to win. After all, he had needed to use his second stream of sword energy to gain a quick victory. Now he only had three such streams left.

Grandpa Ninth’s sword energy has limits. It can kill an early Imperial Sovereign. But it won’t work so well against someone in the mid Imperial Sovereign level....

In order to speed up his recovery, Xu Qing focused on stimulating the violet crystal, all while consuming large amounts of medicinal pills. He worked on recovery all while speeding along at top speed and keeping his senses spread out in all directions. At the same time, he thought about everything that had happened so far in the Fifth Star Ring.

The Fifth Star Ring was a unified place! In that respect, it was very different from the Ninth Star Ring, which was where the Revered Ancient mainland was located.

Based on the map Xu Qing had seen in the Devilbird holy land, Xu Qing knew that there were different factions in the Ninth Star Ring, all of them arrayed around the broken face.

In contrast, the Fifth Star Ring was united. The gods there had been conquered and outlawed. All species were able to practice cultivation. Everyone followed the lead of the cultivators. And there were many powerful experts.

Xu Qing was currently in a remote location near the spot where the south met the west. Yet he had already run into multiple Imperial Sovereigns. That alone went to show how impressive the Fifth Star Ring was.

As far as Xu Qing was concerned, this posed both a challenge and a destined opportunity. It offered both extreme danger and good fortune. Since arriving in the Fifth Star Ring, he had experienced multiple fights with very powerful experts. Each of them brought Xu Qing new enlightenment and understanding. It helped him learn more about the Imperial Sovereign level, and also brought him deeper insights into his own daos.

During his fight with Ling Feng, the guardian of the spirit mine, he came to understand the strengths and weaknesses of his own daos. He had learned about the scale of his cultivation base, and also reminded him that his limits were often set by his own imagination. The grandeur of the five elements was variable and boundless.

Next he fought that city magistrate, which further confirmed what he had learned in the previous battle, and also enabled him to realize that his personal daos could be turned into authority.

And then there was his fight today with this young man. Because of this fight, Xu Qing saw what it was possible to do by developing authority to a higher level. The results could be truly majestic. In the hands of this opponent, wind authority alone was enough to shake all of his five elements. What was more, two authorities could be combined and augmented with an outside object to create an effect like that of a third authority.

There was no way Xu Qing couldn’t feel shaken by all that. Normally speaking, he would have been happy for that fight to go on for longer. It would definitely have provided further tempering and insights. Unfortunately... the way his opponent was acting indicated that danger was on the way.

About an hour later, Xu Qing’s intuition was proved correct.

By means of the Immortal Capital permission medallion, he saw a flickering star appear within the range of his senses, some 5,000,000 kilometers away. This particular star was far brighter than any of the others he had seen up to this point. The moment he saw it, his heart filled with an unprecedented sensation of deep crisis.

What was more, this person had obviously locked onto his location, and was speeding toward him rapidly.

Xu Qing felt a sharp, prickling sensation on his back, and it was growing stronger by the moment. His pupils constricted, and he was breathing heavily as the sensation of crisis grew explosively within him.

Back when he activated the permission medallion, he had briefly glimpsed all of the other medallion-holders in the southern region. They looked like densely packed stars. Though they differed in brightness, he had been able to glance over all of them. But the star he was seeing right now looked different than all the others. Though it was a mere symbol, it filled his heart with dread. And despite being so far away, it was so bright that it seemed blinding.

This person... is extremely strong, with a cultivation base that isn’t even in mid Imperial Sovereign. This person is probably a late Imperial Sovereign! The guy I just killed was waiting for this person to show up!

Given all the conclusions he had reached up to this point, Xu Qing felt lingering trepidation. It was easy to imagine what would have happened if he hadn’t ended that fight so decisively by injuring himself and killing the young man with the birthmark....

For one thing, the range of his medallion wouldn’t have allowed him to detect this person 5,000,000 kilometers away. And if he had been wrapped up in the fighting, that person would eventually have shown up, and he would have been dead. He wouldn’t even have had a chance to flee.

Right now, he was still badly wounded, but at the very least... he wasn’t in a passive position. And he had options. Taking in a deep breath, he unhesitatingly started moving at top speed.

He did everything in his power, even using teleportations, to move in the opposite direction as that blinding star.

Given his current battle prowess, he could kill early Imperial Sovereigns. And with Grandpa Ninth’s sword energy, he could even kill an early Imperial Sovereign in a short moment, though it would result in suffering injuries.

But he wasn’t sure if this stream of sword energy would be enough for him to defeat a mid Imperial Sovereign. And there was little need to mention a terrifying late Imperial Sovereign. Besides, given his injuries, he wasn’t in the position to be fighting.

Unfortunately, even though Xu Qing was moving fast, his pursuer was faster. What was more, it was entirely possible that this person’s medallion range surpassed 5,000,000 kilometers. His opponent would be able to detect all of Xu Qing’s movements. And Xu Qing could tell that this person was moving like a meteor. The distance between them was closing.

A feeling of crisis filled every square inch of Xu Qing’s flesh and blood. Even his soul and his will were filled with a tempest of danger. His blood. His bones. All parts of him were like independent entities screaming at him that he was in danger.

I acted decisively. But in retrospect, I can see that I waited too long.

Xu Qing struggled to control his breathing and forced himself into a state of calm. He knew that moments of life or death weren’t times to get flustered.

Given my current speed, he’ll catch up to me in half an incense stick of time.... With my authority boosted, I could drag the fight out for the time it takes an incense stick to burn, but no more. An incense stick’s worth of time....

Xu Qing summoned a mental image of the map he had bought, and quickly focused on one spot.

The God Blood River! The ferry pilots! The first time you cross the river, it costs six days of longevity. And you’re guaranteed safety!

Without a fragment of hesitation, Xu Qing shifted directions and shot toward the river.

At the same time, his skinless hands flashed in a double-handed incantation gesture, and he coughed up a huge mouthful of blood. A cloud of blood appeared around him, it burst into flames. This blood-burning magic was something Xu Qing had learned from Erniu, and it could significantly increase one’s speed. The downside was that you ended up badly wounded.

Given the danger of the situation, though, Xu Qing didn’t hesitate to use it. In the blink of an eye, he accelerated, vanishing from the spot he had occupied almost as if he had teleported away.

When he reappeared, he was 500,000 kilometers away. Unfortunately... although he was technically in the border region between the west and south, when you considered the entire southern region as a whole, he was still quite a distance away from the God Blood River.

Without any hesitation, he coughed up more blood to make another blood mist. He shot away yet again.

He did the same thing about ten times in a row. In that manner, he traveled more than 5,000,000 kilometers, the result being that his injuries worsened and he was incredibly weak. The upside was that he had managed to keep about 4,000,000 kilometers between himself and his pursuer. To low-level cultivators, that was a distance that would take a long time to cover. But to powerful experts, it was almost nothing.

He used the blood-burning technique several times, then called on his five elements magics, primarily water and fire, using their opposite nature to unleash explosive speed. Then he waved his hand, and the earth churned like the sea, causing huge sections of soil to rise up like walls blocking the sky.

In the blink of an eye, there were hundreds of thousands of such walls of earth. It was profoundly astonishing!

Next came wind!

Xu Qing didn’t have the authority of wind. But his fight with the young man plus the pressure created by the current crisis led him to a sudden understanding. The fundamental properties of wood were similar to that of wind. Both were flexible and had many transformations.[1]

And thus... the power of wood raged and swirled. This was... wood transformed into wind!

Thanks to that, Xu Qing’s speed was bolstered again. As he reached the limits of his fleshly body, heaven and earth rumbled with an astonishing sonic boom.

Yet Xu Qing wasn’t satisfied. Unfortunately, it was obvious that his pursuer had realized what he was doing, and was trying to speed up. As of now, the distance between the two of them was about 2,500,000 kilometers.

Xu Qing could sense the baleful aura behind him, stinging his back. It was like a sun behind him, burning anything and everything. He felt great pressure because of his weakness. Eyes bloodshot, he used some spatial magic. An overlapping grid appeared in the sky. By using that magic, he achieved even more terrifying levels of speed. As he surpassed the limits of his fleshly body, cracks started spreading out over him.

Xu Qing didn’t care. Rumbling sounds echoed out as he once again moved 250,000 kilometers in something like a teleportation. Time magic surrounded him, locking down the passage of time around him. By doing that, he managed to keep his fleshly body whole and intact.

Behind him, the power of fire that Xu Qing had buried in the walls of soil suddenly exploded. They turned into an obstructing force. Though the results were only partially effective, the tiny bit of time it bought was precious to Xu Qing. When every second counts, nothing can be held back.

As Xu Qing pushed himself to his limits and beyond, he shot forward with astonishing speed until he finally caught a glimpse of a boundless river of blood on the horizon.

It was such a mighty river it could span heaven itself. It was actually bigger than a sea. The smell of blood spread out strong in all directions.

Around the time Xu Qing spotted the river, he became so weak that he couldn’t even see clearly. But he still managed to spot a location on the shore where a black ferry boat rested! It looked like an ordinary little boat, and there was a person seated next to it. The person wore a woven rush raincoat and a wide, conical hat. He had a pipe in his hand, which was currently sending smoke curling up into the air.

Xu Qing had no idea what the ferry pilots and their boats looked like. The information in the map hadn’t provided a detailed description. All he knew was that there was only one spot along the river where you could board a ferry boat. He had no time to sit around wondering if this was really a ferry pilot. As soon as he saw the boat, he used the last bit of blood-burning magic he had to shoot forward. An instant later, he was right above the boat.[2]

At the exact same time, the sensation of danger within him reached an explosive level. A terrifying force swept through the sky, and a figure radiating endless fire appeared off in the distance, racing toward him.

He was leveling a fist strike right at Xu Qing.

The Grand Emperor shield appeared. The Grand Emperor shears glittered. There was no need to hold back Grandpa Ninth’s sword energy. Xu Qing also drew... The Emperor’s Sword.

He went all out to fight back.

The might of a late Imperial Sovereign raged. A huge crack snaked out across the Grand Emperor shield, and it was sent spinning off to the side. The Grand Emperor shears suffered a similar fate. The fist strike slammed into them and they exploded. Grandpa Ninth’s sword energy was fierce, but even combined with the shield and the shears, all it could do was slightly weaken the fist strike.

In the end, Xu Qing had to block the blow with The Emperor’s Sword. Rumbling echoed out as Xu Qing shook from head to toe. Massive amounts of flesh and blood were shredded off his body. But in the end, he survived, and used the momentum created by the blow to land on the boat.

The boat vibrated as Xu Qing lay there, gasping for breath, looking like his life force was about to run out. Yet he still kept his hand firmly on the hilt of The Emperor’s Sword. freewebnovel.com

The figure up above didn’t stop for a moment. Approaching, he reached out with his hand... to try to grab Xu Qing.

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed, and he prepared to swallow an object that he had in his mouth.

And yet, just as that hand was about to latch onto him, the ferry pilot in the rush raincoat and conical hat tapped his pipe onto the deck of the boat.

No sound could be heard. But the figure in the air shivered and retracted his hand as he was sent tumbling backward. Some distance away, he came to a stop in midair and resolved into the image of a red-haired young man. Looking fearfully at the ferry pilot, he clasped hands and bowed.

“Senior, I haven’t broken any rules. Although that person landed on your ferry boat, he hasn’t paid the fare. According to the rules... since he hasn’t paid the fare, he isn’t a passenger, and I can kill him!”

“Like hell you can!” the ferry pilot snapped.

His words slammed into the red-haired young man like apocalyptic thunder. The young man staggered backward, shaking, blood pouring out of his mouth.

“This is my boat,” the ferry pilot continued in a growl, “so I decide what happens!” He slowly looked up at Xu Qing. His gaze seemed casual as he looked at The Emperor’s Sword, then at Xu Qing. “Pay up!”

Xu Qing nodded and sent out some of his longevity.

The ferry pilot seemed satisfied. He took some of the longevity, then stood and stretched. An oar appeared out of nowhere, and he put it into the river of blood. Ripples spread out over the surface of the river as the boat slipped away from the shore.

***

The red-haired young man remained in place, his expression grim. He stared at the boat for a long time, his eyes flashing coldly as he considered whether or not he should wait for another ferry pilot to continue the chase in the west. In the end, he didn’t think it was worth it.

For one thing, it would waste one of my chances to use the ferry. What’s more, my clan is in the south. If I went to the west, I’d have to lose a whole sixty-year-cycle to get back.... That guy is pretty badly injured. In fact, he’s almost dead. It’ll be hard for him to recover.

After weighing matters over, the young man turned and left.

***

Out on the river of blood, the ferry pilot looked at Xu Qing lying there.

“That thing in your mouth could heal you if you swallowed it,” he said. “But you held back, you little punk. It was all to make him think you’re not worth chasing. You put a lot of thought into all of this.”

Xu Qing quickly got to his feet and bowed respectfully. “Many thanks for your assistance, Senior.”

“Shut up. I don’t like talking. Especially to people who stink of gods.” The ferry pilot’s gaze lingered on Xu Qing’s empty shoulder for a moment. Without another word, he continued smoking his pipe.

Xu Qing bowed again, went to the stern of the boat, and sat down cross-legged to focus on recovery.

1. The five elements have all sorts of connections to just about everything. When talking about the “environment/climate” associates, wood and wind are connected. You can see that in these five elements charts, and you can find similar information on the Wikipedia page for the five elements. ☜

2. I made an executive decision to add the line about “only one spot” where you could board a ferry boat. This is explicitly spelled out by the author, but not for another 80 chapters or something. There is no special reason for this tidbit to have been left out. It seems like the author just forgot to mention it in this chapter and brought it up later, or possibly he noticed reader comments and provided the explanation later. For me personally, I just couldn’t stop wondering how the heck Xu Qing could randomly just find a ferry boat. Well, he didn’t. So now you know. ☜

The wind blew across the majestic river, causing waves to roll across the god blood. The black boat floated across it. The boat wasn’t moving very fast, yet neither the wind nor the waves did anything to impede its progress. When the boat came, the waves calmed.

The blood rain that fell on the river ceased. It seemed as if this ferry boat was a paramount treasure on this river, and the ferry pilot who operated it apparently had limitless control over the river itself.

And yet, compared to the massive world it was in, this river... was nothing more than a prison for the ferry pilot. After all, there were many ferry pilots, and they came and went depending on when they were convicted and when their sentences ended. It made sense considering that all of them had been convicted of major crimes in the Immortal Capital, and had been sent to this place as a punishment.

That said, taking into consideration the Fifth Star Ring as a whole, there were few people who actually thought of them as being prisoners. No clan would dare to do so, nor would any sect.... Gradually, the ferry boats with their unique fare and offer of safety had become a lifeline to cultivators, and precious protection in key moments.

Xu Qing was the perfect example.

He sat at the stern of the boat, and within his mouth was the flower petal that Grandma Fifth had given him in the Moonrite Region just before he left Revered Ancient. That flower petal could restore him to perfect health, regardless of any injuries he had suffered. He could only use it once, as it was made from the precious life force power of Grandma Fifth herself. It was truly a blessing from her.[1]

Xu Qing didn’t want to use it unless it was completely and utterly necessary.

The Fifth Star Ring is full of danger everywhere.... Given the state of my cultivation base and battle prowess, I need to be very, very careful.

He sat quietly in meditation, relying on the violet crystal to heal himself and slowly grow the skin back over his currently blood-slick flesh. The skin was not really a big deal considering his injuries as a whole. In fact, it only took about a day before he went from looking completely terrifying back to how he had looked before. At the very least, he didn’t look so bedraggled.

Unfortunately, burning so much of his blood had weakened him severely. The final blow he had sustained from that red-haired young man had inflicted a dao injury, and that wasn’t something that would heal in a short time.

It’ll probably take about a month....

Back in the Revered Ancient mainland, taking a month to recover would be a bit dangerous, but Xu Qing would have had plenty of ways to stay safe. But in the unfamiliar Fifth Star Ring, which was full of powerful experts, it was impossible to say how many dangers he might have to deal with in that time.

Therefore, he wanted to take advantage of every moment of his six days on this boat to recover as much as possible. After all, he had paid the fare of six days of life force. Soon enough, he wouldn’t have any true moments of safety at all.

Time passed. Three days went by.

During that time, the ferry pilot would occasionally dip the oar into the water to adjust the course of the boat. Other than that, he just sat at the front of the boat smoking his pipe. He never spoke. Occasionally, he would look up into the sky. It was impossible to determine what he was looking at. The aurora? Something inside the aurora? Or perhaps... he was looking at the void beyond the aurora?

Eventually, another little vortex appeared in the aurora, which was the fourth since Xu Qing boarded. The fourth vortex-day had arrived.

The ferry pilot exhaled a mouthful of smoke, looked away from the sky, and peered into the blood of the river.

“What’s your name, boy?” he asked suddenly.

Xu Qing opened his mouth and was about to say that his name was Sir Firedark.

“Don’t give me a fake name,” the ferry pilot said coolly.

Xu Qing hesitated briefly. “Senior, my name is Xu Qing.”

The ferry pilot closed his eyes and said nothing further.

Xu Qing remembered what the ferry pilot said about how he didn’t like talking. So Xu Qing didn’t say anything further. After all, this ferry pilot was probably the most powerful expert he had ever seen. According to the information provided by the map, if this man was a convict from the Immortal Capital, he was most likely a Lower Immortal. freewebnovel.com

A Lower Immortal was sitting right here in front of him.... It wouldn’t be possible to guess that just from looking at him.... But the fact that he had noticed the clay fox, who was currently dormant, was very telling.

Even as Xu Qing pondered these things, the ferry pilot opened his eyes again and looked up into the sky.

“Where are you from?” he asked.

Xu Qing was surprised, though he tried not to let it show on his face. Keeping calm, he respectfully went into a story based on some places he had learned about from the map.

The ferry pilot listened, and at the end of the story, he grunted a laugh. However, he didn’t pry further into Xu Qing’s past. Instead, he looked Xu Qing up and down as if to assess him.

“You’re a seven-world Smoldering God. You have lots of authority, including that of space and time. Very unusual. You have plenty of unique techniques too. Because of all that, it’s going to be hard to form your eighth and ninth worlds.”

Xu Qing bowed his head. It was really no surprise that someone like this could easily assess all of his daoist magics. He said nothing.

“Considering you have lineaments for your space and time magics,” the ferry pilot continued, “it’s safe to assume you have a plan for your eighth world. So even though the eighth and ninth will be hard, I suppose you just need enough time to work with. Well, do you know what an Imperial Sovereign really is?”

Xu Qing’s heart was beating a bit faster now, as this turn of conversation was a bit of a surprise. It sounded like the ferry pilot was planning to give him some advice.... Xu Qing could guess why this was happening, but had no way to confirm his speculations. And though he wasn’t sure of the details, it was an opportunity he couldn’t just let slip by.

Taking a deep breath, he clasped hands and bowed. “I hope you can clear up my confusion, Senior.”

“The Imperial Sovereign level is after Smoldering God,” the ferry pilot said calmly. “That’s when you form an immortal embryo. That process involves an accompanying immortal dao. Immortal daos are superior to heavenly daos, and they manifest as authority, and by extension, dao lineaments. I suppose you know all of that already.”

Xu Qing listened intently, then nodded in the affirmative.

“But some things in the Fifth Star Ring,” the ferry pilot continued, “are only revealed to cultivators by their clan or sect, after they reach the required level.” He looked at Xu Qing. “What do you think the real point of the Imperial Sovereign level is?”

“The immortal embryo?” he said.

The ferry pilot nodded. “The immortal embryo is also called the undying illusory reality. The illusory represents your soul. The reality represents your fleshly body. And the Imperial Sovereign level is about the process of replacing and merging.”

It was Xu Qing’s first time hearing such things, and he was listening very intently.

“Based on how the process works,” the ferry pilot went on, “the Imperial Sovereign level is divided into the sub-levels of early, mid, and late. The early level involves releasing your soul externally, and using it to form a fleshly body. That is the illusory reality. During that time, the Imperial Sovereign cultivator can be considered strong, but is also weak.

“They’re strong because the external illusion is gradually made real. They come to understand authority, and can control all manner of things. Those abilities eventually reach an inconceivable level. The weakness comes from the fact that reality is concealed by illusion. Therefore, if something can harm reality, they can be killed easily. For example, that stream of sword energy you used serves the function of exterminating reality.

“It’s a formidable stream of sword energy. Though it couldn’t quite kill an undying mid Imperial Sovereign, I can tell that the person who gave it to you is very impressive.”

At this point, the ferry pilot paused for a moment to give Xu Qing time to digest everything up to this point.

Xu Qing was understandably shaken. He had been able to tell before that Grandpa Ninth’s sword energy wouldn’t work very well on a mid Imperial Sovereign, but only now was he getting concrete details from the ferry pilot about why that was. As he thought back to the Imperial Sovereigns he had killed so far, he realized that everything made sense. It was only his previous lack of understanding that prevented him from understanding exactly what was going on.

A short time later, the ferry pilot puffed his pipe again and then continued speaking. “After succeeding with the illusory reality, you can start proceeding through the mid level. That second level involves taking the fleshly body, which was concealed in illusion, and turning it into a soul. That is what is called undying. Imperial Sovereigns of that level can instantly shift between reality and illusion. To some extent, a person like that has no weaknesses, and can be called undying.

“As for the third level, the late level, that requires a dao lineament of authority. The dao lineament is like a thread weaved through the body, taking the illusory, reality, and undying aspects and combining them. Pluck down a star, make it one, and then form the immortal embryo! Success makes you a Quasi-Immortal, also known as a Grand Emperor.”

With this information combined with what he already knew, Xu Qing now felt like he had a clear understanding of the Imperial Sovereign level.

Having an opportunity to get instruction like this was a rare thing, so Xu Qing couldn’t help but ask, “Senior, after the Quasi-Immortal Grand Emperor is the Summer Immortal, right? How do you get to that level?”

The ferry pilot glanced at Xu Qing’s Emperor’s Sword for a moment before saying, “The Quasi-Immortal level is the same as the gods’ Altar God level. The unique thing about that level is canon!

“Canon is the sublimation of dao lineaments of authority. It is power, and will, and essence. It is a continuation of the power of command an immortal developed in life up to that point. As for Lower Immortals....”

The ferry pilot exhaled a stream of pipe smoke. The smoke plus the wide hat made his face almost impossible to see. Yet his voice continued to echo out softly over the river of blood.

“That is the peak for lower star rings. Any such individual can be considered without flaw. Omnipotent. But in the higher star rings where canon reigns supreme, there is further room for growth.”

Xu Qing took a deep breath. Heart pounding, he clasped his hands and bowed again. “Senior, what’s after the Lower Immortal level...?”

The ferry pilot didn’t answer for a long time. When he spoke, his voice was hoarse. “After the Lower Immortals are the Immortal Lords! They who are lords to all other immortals!”

This made Xu Qing think back to something his Eldest Brother had said once. He said he refused to believe that there was no path going beyond Lower Immortal. He said that maybe there were things like Immortal Lords and Immortal Paragons....[2]

I bet Eldest Brother knew the truth even back then.

The ferry pilot was still talking. “Such levels are very difficult to reach. Some people even call them impossible. In all of the Fifth Star Ring, after all the countless years that have passed, there have only been eleven Immortal Lords. They reside in the eleven immortal palaces in the Immortal Capital, and they are all sources of canon.”

The ferry pilot chuckled. “Since we’re talking about this, I might as well tell you about the level after Immortal Lord. It’s Immortal Paragon, and there is only one such individual!

“The Immortal Paragon rules the star ring, and is equivalent to a God Paragon. And the Immortal Paragon in the Fifth Star Ring is actually the only one in all of the thirty-six higher star rings. Before becoming a paragon, he was known as the Fifth Forefather of Humanity.”[3]

Waves surged forth on the God Blood River. The river was so wide that when you looked at it, there seemed no end to it. It stretched from horizon to horizon, filling one with awe and reverence. It was difficult to imagine how many gods must have been killed, and their blood drained, to form this river. It was nothing short of terrifying.

The light cast by the aurora in the dome of heaven caused darkness and brightness to flicker back and forth. As a result, the river almost seemed alive. It seemed to be vying with the aurora for glory. It was a most beautiful and moving image, like a scroll painting.

That painting actually contained evidence of history, bearing testament to the vicissitudes of heaven and earth. It told the story of the war between immortals and gods, and showed how the Fifth Star Ring had ultimately changed. It was deeply significant. freewebnovel.com

Within that blood-colored scroll-painting, a lone ferry boat braved the wind and waves. The voice of the ferry pilot echoed out into the world. His every word resonated like a thunderclap in Xu Qing’s mind, shaking him deeply.

“There is only one Immortal Paragon. The Fifth Forefather of Humanity.”

The words filled Xu Qing’s thoughts, and resulted in the image of an old man to appear in his mind’s eye. It was the same old man Xu Qing had seen in the star chart in the Devilbird holy land. He was seated cross-legged in the Fifth Star Ring. And he was also the old man Xu Qing had met in the outer sea of Revered Ancient.[1]

After a long moment passed, Xu Qing took a deep breath and asked, “Senior, why is that Immortal Paragon... called the Fifth Forefather of Humanity?”

The ferry pilot put his pipe in his mouth, inhaled, then blew out some smoke. “The thirty-six higher star rings are the higher worlds. They each correspond to a different and larger number of lower star rings, which are the lower worlds. Some of the lower star rings have names. Some of them don’t.”

The ferry pilot looked at Xu Qing in a very meaningful way. “The lower world connected to the Fifth Star Ring is one of the ones that didn’t originally have a name. A long time ago, back when the gods ran rampant in the Fifth Star Ring, that lower star ring eventually came to be called the Fifth Lower World.

“All sorts of living beings called it home, but they were slaves to the gods, and were even required to worship them. Eventually there was fighting, rebellion, suppression, emancipation, and apocalypse. They waged war on the gods. The people of the lower world always failed, whereupon the Fifth Lower World would be wiped clean. Then it would all start over again, and the gods would bring about a new crop to harvest.”

As the ferry pilot spoke, his voice rose and fell, becoming like the River of Time itself, flowing through Xu Qing’s perceptions. “Eventually, a human emperor rose up in the Fifth Lower World. His leadership led to an unprecedented golden age in which the immortals fought the gods. The lower waged war against the higher.

“During the war, the emperor of the Fifth Lower World reached the Immortal Paragon level. And then something unexpected happened to the Fifth Star Ring’s God Paragon. The Fifth Star Ring was overthrown, and a new system was established. That’s why he’s called the Fifth Forefather of Humanity.”

With that, the ferry pilot looked up into the canopy of heaven, his face tinged with sorrow.

Xu Qing listened to the story quietly. History often played out like this. As it turned out, the story of the Fifth Star Ring was actually very similar to the story of Revered Ancient. That said, things here had gone more smoothly than back home.

“In that case,” Xu Qing said, “what about the other higher star rings...?”

“None of the wars and rebellions there succeeded,” the ferry pilot continued. “Success was never out of the question, but things always happened that led to failure.”

The ferry pilot shook his head as if thinking of the past. “The thirty-six higher star rings don’t belong to cultivators or immortals. All of them... are the domains of the gods. God and immortal. They are two different paths. And immortals... have limitations that place them one step behind the gods.”

The ferry pilot was speaking in a near growl by this point. “To be precise, once immortals reach the Immortal Paragon level, there’s no path to follow. In all the years that have passed, the Fifth Star Ring’s Immortal Paragon has not made any progress forward. But the gods are different. After the God Paragon level... is the level of Living God!

“Living Gods are not myths. They’re real. However, from ancient times until now, there has only been one. That one god is known as the original Living God. Reportedly, hīs arrival is what led to the creation of the higher and lower worlds. When it comes to that creation story, it’s hard to tell how much is real and how much is false. The history goes back too far for there to be definitive evidence of anything.”

Xu Qing was more shaken by this than by anything else he had heard.

Struggling to control his breathing, Xu Qing began to ask a question, but ended up being interrupted by the ferry pilot, who clearly knew what he had been about to ask.

“Where,” Xu Qing asked, “did that original Living God—”

“Hē left for parts unknown and never returned. As epochs came and went, the thirty-six higher star rings never saw a second Living God, until eventually Desolation showed up in the Ninth Star Ring. Hē was the first god after the original Living God who had any hope of reaching the Living God level. Luckily, hē ended up failing. Otherwise....”

The ferry pilot didn’t go into further detail, but Xu Qing could imagine what he had been about to say.

If Eminent Desolation had succeeded, then all of the thirty-six higher star rings would have been hit by a tempest of godly might. The immortals... would probably not have been able to survive.

Xu Qing sat there digesting everything the ferry pilot had explained.

The ferry pilot had told him many things. He now knew about the breakdown of the Imperial Sovereign level. He understood how strong Quasi-Immortals were. And now he had a clear view of the makeup of the world. It seemed like the ferry pilot had not held one thing back. He had explained everything.

Clearly, the ferry pilot had gone far beyond what his job description entailed. There was actually no reason for him to have gone into all of those explanations. When you coupled that with how the ferry pilot had acted when Xu Qing had been chased to his boat....

Xu Qing had some speculations, but there was no way to confirm them. But he was still inclined to believe... that this ferry pilot had a history with Revered Ancient. In fact, maybe he had even been there. Maybe he was friends with some of the cultivators from Revered Ancient. Xu Qing had no way to figure out the details on his own, but he had noticed how the ferry pilot’s eyes had lingered on The Emperor’s Sword.

After a long moment of silence, Xu Qing blurted, “Senior, have you ever heard of a place called Revered Ancient...?”

The ferry pilot’s eyes narrowed. He said nothing.

Xu Qing hesitated briefly, then sighed in his heart.

Though the ferry pilot had not said anything in response, that reaction in itself provided an answer to the question.

“Senior, some big things have happened in Revered Ancient....”

The ferry pilot continued to smoke his pipe silently.

Xu Qing didn’t say anything. He chose not to continue the conversation.

Time passed, and soon... the six-day voyage was nearing an end. The fare for the voyage was six days of life force, the reason being that the journey took six days.

As the sixth day arrived, Xu Qing spotted the other shore of the majestic God Blood River. He was looking at the western planetary system of the Fifth Star Ring. The water had become calm, with few waves. The boat continued on for a few hours, until the sixth day was almost over.

At that point it reached the shore. The soil was different from the swampy southern region. There was no swamp here. There was only the color red, as if everything contained fire.

“You can debark now,” the ferry pilot said coolly. “If you want to cross the river a second time, the fare won’t be six days of longevity. It’ll be a sixty-year-cycle.”

Xu Qing bowed without a word, then jumped off the boat and onto the shore. He turned back to the boat.

The ferry pilot, clad in his woven rush raincoat and conical hat, was smoking his pipe, and the smoke had gathered around him, yet again obscuring his face.

Thinking back to the six-day journey, Xu Qing ducked his head, clasped hands, and bowed at the waist. “Many thanks, Senior.”

Although the ferry pilot hadn’t said much in the final days of the journey, the information he had imparted early on had been monumental. He had completely opened up the world to Xu Qing. As far as Xu Qing was concerned, that was an immense show of kindness.

His bow was completely and utterly sincere. Straightening from his bow, he turned and flew off into the distance.

After Xu Qing was gone, the ferry pilot looked up in the direction he had disappeared.

“So, that stubborn fellow Swordsage finally perished, huh...?”

His voice contained a bit of reminiscence. A moment passed, and he sighed. Revered Ancient.... It’s been a long time since I heard that name. I have the feeling nobody in Revered Ancient remembers who I am at this point.... I’ve surely been erased from the histories there....

The ferry pilot lifted his hand and looked at his palm. There in his palm was a magical symbol that looked like a human face. It emanated a very gruish aura. If Xu Qing had been there, he would have recognized it.... Astonishingly, that face-shaped symbol was... an immortal skill![2]

As Xu Qing flew through the sky in the western region of the Fifth Star Ring, Starfire spoke into his ear.

“That guy... was really scary! The moment he looked at you I was convinced he was going to grab me and stomp me to death! Xu Qing, you brought me to a really, really horrible place!” Starfire was feeling very jumpy. That was especially true when crossing the God Blood River, during which time shē had been shaking in terror. “Ah, whatever. I’ll just go back to sleep I guess....”

Shē once again retracted hēr aura.

Xu Qing wasn’t really sure what to say to Starfire. He had explained from the beginning that he was going to a place that didn’t welcome gods. Apparently Starfire hadn’t really believed him.

After a bit of hesitation, he decided to offer another warning. “Things are only going to get more dangerous....”

Starfire’s aura shrank down even more on itself. Starfire would never behave like this in Revered Ancient, which seemed to indicate that the ferry pilot really had frightened hēr.

Xu Qing couldn’t help but think back to what the ferry pilot looked like.

Who exactly was he...?

Unfortunately, there was no answer to his question. After a while, he put the matter aside and checked his map for information about the western planetary system.

The west was much weaker than the other three regions. And the orthodox organization here, the Dao Immortal Sect, was in dire straits. The heavenly inspector in the west didn’t care much about mortal affairs, nor the development of the sect. In fact, the heavenly inspector didn’t care about much at all. As a result, the cultivators in the sect had developed a very lackadaisical attitude.

However, because of that, there were more clans and other organizations here than the other three regions, and they were always fighting each other in the hopes of gaining supremacy. After looking over the information, Xu Qing reviewed the details of the Shining Star from this area.

Of the eight Shining Stars, the weakest was the apprentice of the Dao Immortal Sect’s heavenly inspector.

Li Mengtu.... One unique thing about this clan is that all direct bloodline clan members have the character “tu” in their name. His cultivation base is in the early Imperial Sovereign level, and he has four types of authority. However, because he has the legacy of his clan’s gruish magical technique, as well as training from his Master, he was able to kill a mid Imperial Sovereign.

Xu Qing looked around at the western lands.

This place seems a lot quieter than the south. I should be able to recover here. But it’s not a good place to temper myself via battle. Right now, I need to find a good place to hole up and get better. As for what happens after that... I’ll have to play it by ear.

Eyes filling with determination, he sped off.
