The ancient voice which responded came from beneath the lake. “Aurora, there’s no need to worry so much about the affairs of the younger generation.”

The voice was hoarse, and seemed to contain an indescribable melancholy. As the voice spoke, the water beneath the ice rippled, and Xu Qing could see a majestic figure like a god. He was enormous, taking up the greater part of the lake, with indistinguishable facial features, as if a veil obscured them. As for the eyes in that face, they were like suns casting silver light.

Looking down at the figure in the lake, Immortal Lord Aurora shook his head somberly. “He’s responsible for everything that happened, from beginning to end. Half a year ago, I simply asked him to come here to work on his cultivation. I had no idea what my unfilial son was really thinking. He wasn’t interested in cultivation at all, Daoist Brother. Instead, he was interested in your lovely daughter.

“Thankfully, the interest seemed to be mutual, and there was no force involved. But despite how they got along, eventually they had a misunderstanding. Of course, it’s not good for us elders to interfere blithely. Furthermore, though my unfilial son has made mistakes, he does have a sense of responsibility. Therefore, Daoist Brother Nineshores, I’ve brought him here today to formally propose marriage.

“I hope that these two young ones can journey forward together as daoist partners and close companions. Since they both pursue the dao, I think both you and I can agree that they will eventually become immortals together. I think that would be a good ending to the story.”

Before Immortal Lord Aurora’s words finished echoing in the area, he waved his right hand. Four items appeared out of nowhere.

“Here are four betrothal gifts,” Immortal Lord Aurora said calmly. “First is the collected blood and marrow left behind when the two gods Lohn and Menghin perished here in the Fifth Star Ring. It includes a bit of thēir future discarnate wills, as well as thēir secrets. I know that you’ve longed for this item for a very long time, and I managed to secure it for you only a few days ago.”

His words were very humble, and they downplayed his own importance. It could only be imagined the astonishing price that would have to be paid for an item that an Immortal Lord longed for. When the item was produced, the silver eyes of the face behind the veil glittered.

“Second is a pair of empty jade slips formed from my own soul blood. The first one is waiting to be filled out by you next month, Daoist Brother Nineshores. Inscribe it however you wish, and it will be considered an order from me.

“As for the other jade slip, Daoist Brother Nineshores, you can inscribe it with any item in my immortal palace. As soon as you do, all karma on that item will be erased, and ownership of it will be transferred to you.”

Xu Qing was visibly moved. The first item surpassed his comprehension. But the set of jade slips were incredible. The one which could be inscribed with orders was essentially like an imperial edict. After all, in a month, Aurora would be succeeding Nineshores and taking over the throne. The future era would be that of Aurora, so to leave behind a blank imperial edict was profoundly significant. The same held for items in the immortal palace. And what was even more significant was that there was no time limit attached to either item.

These gifts showed an immense amount of sincerity! At the bottom of the lake, Nineshores opened his mouth as if to speak.

Before he could, Immortal Lord Aurora kept talking. “The fourth gift is of little value. It is my son’s birthdate characters.”[1]

Immortal Lord Aurora waved his hand, and a red piece of paper flew out, upon which was written eight characters. Xu Qing looked over and confirmed that it was the birthdate of his host. All of these things combined suddenly filled him with a deep sense of paternal love.

Having accomplished these things, Immortal Lord Aurora clasped hands and bowed deeply to the lake.

Considering the gifts, the status of the person involved, and the bow, Nineshores felt compelled to speak, and could not remain at the bottom of the lake. A sigh echoed out, which turned into innumerable threads that rose up through the water.

They were made of the secrets of the world, intangible as they pierced through the layer of ice. After coming through the ice... they transformed from incorporeal to corporeal. A middle-aged cultivator stood there now, clad in a blue daoist robe, pulsing with the demeanor of a transcendent being.

He stood right in front of Aurora and looked him in the eyes. He nodded. Then he extended his right hand. The blood, the jade slip that was the imperial order, and the piece of paper with the birthdate all flew up to him. He put them away. As for the jade slip that could be filled in with an item from the immortal palace, he flicked it to Xu Qing.

Xu Qing caught it.

“In a month, you’ll marry my daughter. Going forward, you will no longer be the son of Aurora. You’ll be the son-in-law of Nineshores.”

Xu Qing inclined his head, clasped his hands, and bowed deeply.

Immortal Lord Aurora smiled as if an immense weight had been lifted off his shoulders. A rare smile appeared on his face. He looked at Nineshores, who was in fact his lifelong friend. They had grown up together, furthered their cultivation together, fought enemies together, and faced death on numerous occasions. The mixture of steel and blood had caused a deep friendship to form....

Each would have died for the other. And the truth was that when they were young, they had laughed about what it would be like when they had children in the future. Maybe those children would be like brothers. Or maybe they would become daoist partners.

Mind filled with such thoughts, Aurora quietly clasped hands, then turned to leave.

Xu Qing got to his feet, bowed, and left, a complicated expression on his face.

Nineshores stood there quietly as he watched the two of them walk away into the distance. Eventually, he sighed in his heart. I know you’re going to do something that will shake heaven and earth.... Aurora. Oh, Aurora. You can truly be called a filial son to the Immortal Paragon. And to that child, you are a compassionate father!

But for you to be stuck in the middle must be pure bitterness. Perhaps from the moment Lanxi perished, you no longer wished to linger in this world.[2]

Nineshores sighed softly, then blurred, turning again into countless threads that passed back through the ice and sank to the bottom of the lake.

***

After leaving the Nineshores Grotto-Heaven, father and son continued on through heaven and earth. A gentle breeze stirred Immortal Lord Aurora’s hair, and did the same to Xu Qing’s host. Neither of them spoke.

Xu Qing wasn’t sure if it was a misperception or not, but it seemed to him that the wind was taking away some of Immortal Lord Aurora’s coldness. His apathy seemed to be slowly fading away. And it had all started... when Immortal Lord Nineshores nodded. The weight which had lifted off him at that moment must have been immense.

Xu Qing soon realized they weren’t going back to the immortal palace. Instead, they were getting closer and closer to a location familiar to Xu Qing.

Eventually, a vast sea of golden sand appeared ahead. It looked like an actual sea, full of dazzling waves, shining gloriously in the sun. It seemed like a dream or an illusion.

Xu Qing had been to this desert before. However, he had seen a version that existed countless years later. This version was from much earlier in the timescape.

That which separated the two was the name of the desert itself.

Time.

“When you were little,” Immortal Lord Aurora said softly, “you always asked me about your mother.”

As they walked out over the desert, the Immortal Lord didn’t seem like an immortal anymore. Apparently, this desert was profoundly significant to him. Now that he was back, he suddenly seemed a lot older.

“I never told you much. But you’ve grown up and are about to get married. Soon you’ll have your own wife. Therefore... I brought you here. This is the spot where your mother’s soul faded away. This is the only place that has anything of her left.”

1. Birthdate characters are a combination of the Heavenly Stems and Earthly Branches that describe the time, date, month, and year of a person’s birth, primarily used in fortune-telling. And since I’m sure some of you will want to go back and check, we did recently come to find out about a set of eight characters that clearly described a specific date and time. That was in chapter 1146, with a detailed explanation of calendar-related stuff in 1147. As of now, we don’t have enough information to determine if the date mentioned back there is the same as the one here, but it seems highly likely. ☜

2. Lanxi: This is a given name without a surname. Lan means “orchid” and Xi means “evening tide.” ☜

Mother...? As Xu Qing walked along behind Immortal Lord Aurora, he looked at the desert and listened to the story.

Perhaps it was some sort of resonance with his host’s body, or perhaps it was the word ‘mother’ itself. Either way, he suddenly found himself thinking about his own past.

In his mind’s eye, he saw Peerless City in the Revered Ancient mainland. He remembered his dad and mom there in the city. Those were good times. But then the blood rain fell.

He thought back to his father and mother. Perhaps he had traveled too far and experienced too many things, because all of a sudden he realized that all that remained of his parents in his memory was an outline. However, that outline exuded warmth. It didn’t matter how far he traveled or what he experienced, that impression would never go away. It would always be there in his mind.

People can’t determine who it is that they will see last in life. But the first people to accompany them are always the parents.

Mother....

At the same time, his host was also wrapped in such thoughts. In the memories of his host, he could see only the vague outline of a mother.... It was just like Xu Qing thinking about his past.

As of this moment, the two of them were in complete resonance. The resonance turned into ripples, flowing through the sea of the heart, stirring time and spreading out into the desert. It became part of the desert.

Immortal Lord Aurora’s voice drifted across the Desert of Time.

“Your mother and I got to know each other back in our hometown. She was my Junior Sister, in other words, the seventh apprentice of your grandfather. Back in those days, there was a sun and moon, but they looked different than they do now.”[1]

Immortal Lord Aurora was talking to Xu Qing, but also seemed to be simply recalling the past. As he spoke, he seemed to get older, and to sink further into reminiscence. “Back then, our hometown was just one of many captive minor worlds in the Fifth Star Ring that belonged to the gods. It was a life in which you worshiped gods, were enslaved by them, and had nothing to look forward to except death.

“Naturally speaking, the sun and moon overhead were both gods. I guess it’s most accurate to say that the light of the sun and moon came into our minor world. Their names were the most paramount godly names in the entire minor world. Clearbright and Fyreblaze. Those times were full of pain and bitterness. But with your mother there, I was happy.”

Immortal Lord Aurora spoke softly, and Xu Qing followed, listening quietly. He knew that now was a moment in which he should pay attention respectfully.

“We furthered our cultivation together. We grew up together. And eventually we ran into Nineshores.”

Immortal Lord Aurora shook his head as he sank further into memory. “His personality back then was much the same as it is now. He was quiet. He liked to observe things and keep records. Your mother called him the Great Scribe. He actually liked that, and it’s what we called him for many years. So stupid.” Aurora smiled.

“And so, time passed.... What happened later is there in the history books. You know all about that. In Dao Finale of the God Epoch, your grandfather led our minor world in a great war against the gods. It was a desperate war. More desperate than you can imagine....

“You were born during that time. But your mom didn’t want you to see all the chaos, so she sealed you away. We agreed that we would wait until the war was over and the world had become magnificent before we unsealed you. Then you would be able to see lands full of beauty and peace. With no gods. We wanted you to have the most wonderful life possible.”

Aurora’s voice continued to echo in the Desert of Time, full of both reminiscence and grief. “The war lasted for many years. But eventually it ended, and we cultivators had fully risen to prominence. We crushed all of those high and mighty gods. The sun and the moon in the sky perished, and we replaced them with our own versions.

“Unfortunately... I lost someone forever during that time. Your mother died.”

Xu Qing listened quietly. This was someone else’s story, yet for whatever reason, perhaps the resonance that had sprung up, Xu Qing could feel his host’s sorrow, a well as Aurora’s grief.

“For certain reasons, I fell into a deep slumber that lasted for 10,000 years. By the time I woke up, it was impossible to change what had happened. The canon of space-time had reached its limit.... 3,333 years. That’s the ultimate limit of space-time in this star ring. When you were sealed away, your mother and I were both there. But when it came time to unseal you, only I was left.”

Aurora suddenly stopped walking.

Xu Qing saw a sea of flowers. It was an illusory sea, filled with endless gorgeous orchids blooming in the middle of the desert. It was consummately beautiful. It was hard to imagine how there could be a sea of orchids in the middle of a desert. At the very least, Xu Qing knew that when he visited this desert far in the future, there had been nothing like it. Apparently, this was a secret buried in the depths of the desert.

The exquisite orchids were of different shapes and sizes. Some looked like fluttering butterflies. Others resembled soaring immortal cranes. All of them had unique fragrances.

As Xu Qing and Immortal Lord Aurora arrived, the sun shone through the scattered clouds onto the sea of orchids, and the golden beams of light added a further sense of mystery and romance.

A faint breeze stirred the flowers. It all seemed like a dream. And then it almost seemed like an immortal fairy had appeared in the flowers, and was looking at the two of them. A faint murmuring sound could be heard, like gentle laughter.

Immortal Lord Aurora looked at the sea of flowers, and the immortal fairy from his memories. He also laughed softly. Striding to the edge of the sea of flowers, he knelt down and produced a handful of seeds from within the fold of his robe. As of this moment, he wasn’t the soon-to-be most respected person in the Fifth Star Ring. He was not a ruler of countless immortals, with an astonishing cultivation base. He was just an ordinary person thinking about his deceased wife.

He was now planting the seeds in the desert. They would definitely bloom eventually. “Your mother’s name had the character ‘orchid’ in it, and her favorite flower was always the immortal orchid. It’s a flower that cannot be tainted with the aura of gods, otherwise it withers.... And yet, that type of flower never disappeared from our minor world, despite the proliferation of mutagen. Because after it withers, it can bloom again.

“We had always hoped that, after the war was over and everything was beautiful, we could find a place to plant some immortal orchids, and turn them into a sea that bloomed year round. Over the years, I’ve always made sure to plant some more when I come here. Gradually, they’ve turned into a sea.”

Smiling, Immortal Lord Aurora patted the soil over the seeds he had just planted. Then he sat down and looked out at the flowers. He said nothing, yet the warm smile remained on his face.

Xu Qing quietly walked over, sat down next to Immortal Lord Aurora, and joined him in looking out at the flowers.

Time passed.

When evening approached, Immortal Lord Aurora spoke again.

“You’ve grown up,” he said softly. “And you’re about to get married. In the future, I’ll be very busy, so remember to come back here every year and plant some more orchids for your mother. Let’s make sure there’s always a sea of flowers here.”

Mixed emotions filled Xu Qing. He was fully aware that in a month, Immortal Lord Aurora was going to die, as was his host body.

Years in the future, there would no longer be a sea of orchids here. Perhaps that was why he had not seen any flowers when he passed through this desert. The sea of flowers had long since withered up as time passed.

But he still nodded.

Aurora smiled, and in uncharacteristic fashion, reached out and tousled his son’s hair. “I want you to remember something. Your mother wasn’t able to accompany you through life, nor will your own children be able to stay with you all the time. Only your daoist partner... will keep you company forever. You have to take care of her. Don’t be like me.... Don’t lose the person you love.”

With that, Aurora stood up and looked at Xu Qing. “Do you remember that story I used to tell you when you were young? About the night?”

Xu Qing nodded and quietly said, “When night falls, don’t go to see you.”

That saying was implanted firmly in the memories of Young Lord Aurora. It was something that Immortal Lord Aurora had told him many times. It made Xu Qing think about the reflection beneath the ice lake.... Based on his memories, Immortal Lord Aurora always came to him during the day....

Aurora smiled and nodded, then looked at the deepening evening. “It’s about to get dark. Let’s go back.”

With that, Aurora took a step forward. Everything blurred. A moment later, the desert was gone, and so was the sea of flowers.

Xu Qing was back in Young Aurora Hall, in the exact spot where he had left it. It was almost as if everything that had just happened was an illusion. Immortal Lord Aurora was nowhere to be seen.

As for the sky... when Xu Qing left, it was bright. Right now, night was falling. Darkness covered the lands.

The moon rose.

***

Deep beneath the immortal palace was a secret chamber, brightly lit with lamps. Immortal Lord Aurora was there, striding forward. As he passed, the lamps behind him went out.

Night fell outside and his white clothing began to turn dark. Before long, his robe was pitch black. The kind look on his face became replaced with something vicious and wicked. He started trembling, and his pace faltered. However, he managed to walk all the way to the end of the cave. There, he entered a prison cell.

The moment he was inside, countless magical symbols formed chains that wrapped around him, both blessing him and sealing him. All of the light went out, and everything became pitch black.

Within that darkness, groans echoed out, along with the clink of chains.

1. Specifically this is the paternal grandfather, so that would be Immortal Lord Aurora’s father, who we know is the Immortal Paragon. ☜

It was night at Young Aurora Hall, and the lanterns shone brightly.

Inside, Xu Qing was thinking about everything that just happened with Immortal Lord Aurora. On the road, Aurora was an Immortal Lord. Outside the Nineshores Grotto-Heaven, he was a father. And in the Desert of Time, he was a lonely man who had lost the love of his life. By the time night fell and he was back in the immortal palace, he was back to being an Immortal Lord.

Before this event, Xu Qing had considered Immortal Lord Aurora to be little more than a symbol. Granted, the imp in the second world had called himself a scrap of discarnate will from Immortal Lord Aurora. But whether or not that was true would require further investigation. From the very beginning until now, Xu Qing had had his doubts. That was why, to him, the words ‘Immortal Lord Aurora’ had been just that: words.

But everything he had experienced just now, and the different versions of Aurora that he had seen, all painted a very different picture. Without even realizing, he had come to view Aurora as a real and complex person.

And now I’m getting an inkling of what’s going to happen in a month....

Otherwise, how was it possible to explain how Aurora had essentially entrusted his son to another like an orphan? And what explanation was there for what he had said in the desert? However, even as some of the puzzle pieces clicked into place in his mind, more questions and suspicions proliferated.

Immortal Lord Aurora already had space-time canon, and has pushed it much closer to completion than I have. He has to know what’s coming in the future. It’s not going to come as a surprise to him.

So what’s going to happen in a month that will cause the Immortal Paragon to interfere? Why does the historical record call it a rebellion? And why am I instructed not to go see him at nighttime? Does it have something to do with that sinister, black-garbed version of him I saw under the lake?

Furthermore, he’s made all sorts of arrangements, including entrusting his son to someone else. So why does his son die in a month? What’s more, why does everyone else in the immortal palace die as well? Why does the Immortal Paragon wipe out every living being here?

Even stranger, why does the palace get left behind to exist for such a long time afterward....

There were too many questions swirling in Xu Qing’s mind. Even after much analysis, he didn’t come up with any good answers.

I’ll see it all play out in a month!

Xu Qing looked up at the moon in the night sky, then entered the main hall and sat down cross-legged. For the time being, he put Immortal Lord Aurora out of mind, and instead focused his attention on how to create waves in space-time.

For most people, the space-time of the fourth world was about the people and the scenery. But to someone like Xu Qing with his space-time canon, things were completely different. To his senses, the space-time here was fixed, like a pool of stagnant or even frozen water. It was still, with no fluctuations or ripples much less waves. Directly tampering with it wasn’t possible, even with Xu Qing’s space-time canon.

I need more elements at play. They need to be like rocks, thrown one after another to disturb the stagnant water....

***

Time passed.

The sound of music and soft laughter drifted out from the Hundred Flowers Palace. The melodious sounds fused with the darkness. Even Xu Qing, who was still seated cross-legged in the main hall, could hear.

The laughter of the fox maiden was particularly clear. Clearly, the fox maiden was having a good time regardless of whether Xu Qing was there or not.

Eventually, dawn arrived. The shining sun rose, casting its light out everywhere.

The melodious sounds faded away, and soon, a voice spoke outside of the hall.

“Greetings, Young Lord, and welcome back to the palace!”

It was none other than Li Mengtu, who was playing the role of Young Lord Aurora’s study partner, Zhong Chi. Hurrying forward, he entered the hall and bowed. Of course, he had a lot of speculations about what was going on, considering that he hadn’t seen Young Lord Aurora for an entire day. He had searched Young Aurora Hall high and low, all to no avail. He couldn’t help but be very curious about where the young lord had gone off to. Though he had a general idea of what happened in this time period, there was no way that he could know the details of what happened every hour of every day.

Xu Qing looked up at Li Mengtu and said, “You’re late. I actually came back last night.”

Li Mengtu carefully replied, “Young Lord, might I ask how yesterday fared for you...?”

Xu Qing’s expression remained placid as, instead of answering the question, he simply stood and casually said, “Come with me to the Magic Legacy Pavilion.”

And with that, he walked out. Given that he had the opportunity in this place, he was not going to miss out on the chance to go to the immortal palace’s Magic Legacy Pavilion and see what kind of magical techniques were available in this time period.

Li Mengtu, of course, hurried to follow.

The sun was still rising as Xu Qing made his way through the immortal palace. The cultivators he encountered along the way didn’t think much of Young Lord Aurora. But given his important status, all of them bowed in greeting.

Li Mengtu hurried along, looking like he wanted to say something, but ultimately biting his tongue.

As the Magic Legacy Pavilion appeared off in the distance, Xu Qing calmly said, “Zhong Chi, you’ve been acting differently lately.”

Li Mengtu’s guard instantly went up, but he didn’t show it. Smiling wryly, he said, “You’re very observant, Young Lord. There’s something that’s been bothering me lately, and though I tried to keep it inside, I guess you noticed the clues.”

“What is it?” Xu Qing asked calmly.

Li Mengtu hesitated. “It’s Li the Chosen! Young Lord, please don’t accuse me of tattling, but I just have to say that he’s really a disgrace! Didn’t you say that he should work at your beast ranch? Well he didn’t go there at all! In fact, he just disappeared altogether. He hasn’t even been seen at the university anymore!”

Xu Qing’s facial expression didn’t change in response to this information. He just turned to look at Li Mengtu. “Presumably you know what’s going on?”

The look in Xu Qing’s eyes caused Li Mengtu to shiver inwardly. The truth was that he had already gotten to the bottom of the situation. The reason he hadn’t mentioned something sooner was that he wasn’t entirely sure how the young lord would react. But given how terrifying Xu Qing’s gaze was, Li Mengtu didn’t dare to hide any of the details.

“I heard that after he returned to the university that day, he got into an argument with one of the teachers. The end result was that the teacher punished him by sending him into seclusion for three months.”

The real reason Li Mengtu was revealing this information was self-interest. He had come to the conclusion there was an eighty to ninety percent chance that Li the Chosen was also an outsider. Though he didn’t know who it was, he was certain that they were trying to alter history. That, of course, aligned with his own goal. Fundamentally speaking, he wanted Li the Chosen to succeed. That would give him the perfect point of reference to learn from and imitate.

Li the Chosen had lived up to expectations to an extent. Historically speaking, he had gone into seclusion after being defeated in the duel. But that had changed when Young Lord Aurora appointed him to serve at his beast ranch.

Obviously, someone else had interfered to maintain historical accuracy. Although there had been a slight deviation, in the end, things worked out the same.

As for who had interfered, Li Mengtu’s initial guess was that it was Fourth True Monarch! Unfortunately, whoever had taken that identity obviously had a major advantage. And if he could make sure Li the Chosen failed to alter history, then he would surely do the same to Li Mengtu. Therefore, Li Mengtu was hoping that Young Lord Aurora could do something about the situation.

If this was the real Young Lord Aurora, then he obviously wouldn’t have had any idea what was going on. But it was Xu Qing, who knew exactly what was happening.

Li Mengtu is trying to make use of my power. Although Li the Chosen’s story hasn’t played out exactly the way it did in history, the fact remains that someone corrected things so they got back on track. Whoever took the identity of Fourth True Monarch is obviously quite skilled.

Xu Qing thought about it for a moment. Whoever it was, they were using Li the Chosen as a tool to vie with Xu Qing. So far, both sides had succeeded and failed to varying degrees.

I don’t want to interfere any further. When it comes to Li the Chosen, I already made my move and lost. There’s no need to rile things up further. After all, keeping my true identity hidden is the best way to acquire good fortune here.

Eyes narrowing, Xu Qing continued onward toward the Magic Legacy Pavilion. Once inside, he started skimming through the various magical techniques, all the while continuing to analyze the situation.

Protecting my identity is the most important thing. As far as I can tell, no one suspects me at all, including the people playing the roles of Zhong Chi, Li the Chosen, Nineshores’ daughter Zhou Linshan, and Fourth True Monarch.

As far as they’re concerned, it’s not even possible for someone to have taken the identity of Young Lord Aurora. The only people who can come to the fourth world are either Quasi-Immortals or people who have canon or canon treasures.

Forgetting the ones I’ve already identified as outsiders, there should be at least four or five others here in the immortal palace. And there should be a few of them who are also trying to make waves in space-time. They are the rocks I need!

Xu Qing put down the jade slip he had been looking at and picked up a new one. As he scanned it, he continued thinking.

This entire thing is like one big game of Go. Fourth True Monarch wants to stop the ones breaking the rules. The rocks. And I... want to secretly help and protect them. Of course, they’re also going to be focused on taking care of themselves.

Li the Chosen already lost, the reason being that he got too anxious. Of course, part of that was because of the identity he acquired. He only had one shot on that specific day. If he didn’t take that opportunity, he wouldn’t have had another.

Unfortunately, everyone else has remained hidden too well. If I can’t figure out who they are, I have no way to help or protect them. So how is Fourth True Monarch finding them?

Time passed quickly as he pondered matters and simultaneously looked through the techniques. Around the time the sun was setting, he left the Magic Legacy Pavilion and returned to Young Aurora Hall. By that time, he had come up with a plan.

I don’t need to find all of the rocks. I just need to make sure they’re all staying cautious and on guard. I guess making them feel threatened would do the trick. As for Fourth True Monarch.... I’m still hidden, while he’s out in the open, although not completely. If I could unmask him completely, and force him to break his own rules, that would be perfect!

As Xu Qing sat down in the main hall, he closed his eyes and sent his divine will to the Hundred Flowers Palace. There, the fox maiden was lounging lazily and chatting with the other beautiful women. Suddenly, her eyebrows shot up, and she groaned inwardly. That naughty man has really grown a spine. I almost can’t believe he’s giving me orders.... That said, seeing him so domineering just makes me like him more.

The fox maiden licked her lips and laughed softly.

***

For a few days, things were quiet in the Aurora Immortal Palace. But then two rumors spread like wildfire.

According to the first rumor, outsiders had possessed certain cultivators in the immortal palace. They were currently under cover plotting and scheming, and there were quite a few of them!

The second rumor was about Fourth True Monarch. Supposedly....

“Fourth True Monarch was possessed by the leader of the outsiders!”

Xu Qing’s goal was very simple. The outsiders he had not yet identified were extraordinary individuals. Not one of them could be considered a simpleton. Unless it was absolutely necessary, they weren’t going to risk revealing themselves the way Li the Chosen had. And unless they did reveal themselves, finding them would be as difficult as fishing a needle from the sea. Each of them had their own unique goals and plans, making it that much more difficult to identify them. And if they knew someone was coming after them, they would work even harder to maintain their cover.

It was less of an issue for those who wanted to create waves in space-time. Xu Qing was fairly confident that he would be able to find them eventually. After all, they would eventually be like flames in the night, easy to spot. Good examples were Li the Chosen, Li Mengtu as Zhong Chi, and Zhou Linshan, who was the daughter of Nineshores, commonly referred to as Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix. All of them were using him as an anchor point.

Unfortunately, the whole process would take time. What was more, it was hard to say how many of the outsiders wanted to cause waves in space-time, and how many of them wanted to protect the status quo and just watch things play out as they did historically speaking. If they truly just played the role of spectators, it was going to be difficult to identify them.

All he could do was keep looking. Otherwise....

Since I have no way to immediately locate the hidden outsiders, then the first rumor I spread will at least tell them they need to exercise greater cautions. That way, even if I don’t find them, at least Fourth True Monarch will have to work a lot harder to do the same. As for the second rumor....

Inside Young Aurora Hall, Xu Qing was looking out at the sky.

It will force him even more into the open. The rumors could directly blow his cover.

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered. It didn’t matter whether or not the inhabitants of this time period believed the rumors. The important thing was that other outsiders be given some serious food for thought. They were being sent a message. At the same time, he was already creating a wave in history.

In the situation with Li the Chosen, I won the first half of the round, but lost to Fourth True Monarch in the second half. As for the current situation, I don’t yet know how Fourth True Monarch is going to react. If he gets bogged down trying to prove he’s not an outsider, all the better for me.

Right now, the most important thing for him to do was stay hidden and keep his eyes open. He wanted to see how the immortal palace would react to the tempest caused by the rumors, and what the ramifications might be.

In addition to the advantage I have because I’m still in hiding, there’s a second upside I have in this game of history....

He looked in the direction of the Hundred Flowers Palace. Nobody had any idea that Starfire was here! Everyone else who had entered the fourth world was leaving clues behind that astute observers would eventually be able to notice. But not Starfire. Shē had not left any clues at all, and thus, shē was going to be a huge asset to Xu Qing.

***

A few days later....

The rumors brought mixed results. Though they spread far and wide in the immortal palace, in the end, the inhabitants of the time period found the rumors to be laughable. After all, this was the Aurora Immortal Palace!

It was true that the different Immortal Lords in the Fifth Star Ring had all come from different minor worlds, and didn’t always get along perfectly. There were occasional conflicts. But... in a general sense, they were all unified around common ideals.

Even more important, the Immortal Paragon was always there, mighty above all else. And he wouldn’t possibly allow significant conflicts to arise between the Immortal Lords. Because of that, most people felt that it didn’t matter one way or another if there were outsiders possessing certain individuals in the immortal palace.

Beyond that, astute individuals could tell that the rumors had obviously been spread for a specific reason. And that was especially true considering that they directly called out Fourth True Monarch. Most of the cultivators in the palace chose to just wait and see what happened.

In contrast, the outsiders in hiding were exceptionally vigilant. Although they had different perspectives, all of them were able to come up with valid speculations about what was really going on.

At the moment, Li Mengtu in the guise of Zhong Chi was listening in on a group of immortal palace cultivators conversing about the subject. Of course, he was as on guard as ever. This feels like an actual war.... Just as I suspected, Fourth True Monarch is an outsider. The real question now is who started spreading the rumors. Who warned everybody? I wonder if that Diling fellow managed to get my message to Xu Qing. Did he make it here to the fourth world?

In a guest hall in the south of the immortal palace, Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix sat cross-legged, listening to a handmaiden deliver a report. Though she looked like she was bored, she was actually paying very close attention. Fourth True Monarch? No wonder he suddenly showed up to that duel between Li the Chosen and Young Lord Aurora. Li the Chosen was completely exposed at that point. However, it seems like Fourth True Monarch wants to prevent any changes to history, which means the two of us don’t have any conflict with each other. I do need to stay careful, though.

There were people thinking similar thoughts all throughout the immortal palace.

It was the same in the sword furnace. Hordeslayer and Rampart were so perfectly hidden it didn’t seem anyone could find them. However, after Fourth True Monarch had come to them, the brothers had been trying to figure out where they went wrong. Unfortunately, they lacked clues to work with. And then the rumors reached them....

“Someone’s targeting him,” Rampart said via divine will.

“Let them fight,” replied Hordeslayer with a cold snort. “It has nothing to do with us. We can just patiently wait for time to pass until the sword embryo is at its peak state. The main thing I’m wondering about now is who started the rumors.”

***

Zhou Zhengli was in True Monarch Hall, looking at Sir Star Ring, who was seated a short distance away. Keeping his voice low, he said, “There’s a distinct possibility that this is the work of Li the Chosen. But it’s also possible that Sir Vilespirit is responsible! Either way, the result is that we’re in a passive position now.”

“There’s no need for alarm,” Sir Star Ring replied calmly. “You’re falling right into the trap of whoever’s orchestrating this. What’s more... you’re still forgetting someone. No one we know would do this. He has to be the one behind it all.”

Zhou Zhengli thought back to that person he’d seen with Li Mengtu before they’d all entered the immortal palace. “You’re talking about that guy we saw at the entrance? The one who has canon but isn’t one of the Shining Stars?”

“Exactly,” Sir Star Ring said. He looked out the door of the hall and into the sky, his eyes glittering menacingly. “If I just ignore the rumors, I won’t have to waste time trying to prove who I am. A person with an identity like mine wouldn’t pay attention to such rumors anyway.

“The rumors don’t matter. What matters is finding the rumor monger! Thankfully, the act of spreading these rumors has revealed a bit about who this person is. I already have a theory.” Sir Star Ring’s gaze shifted... to the east, toward Young Aurora Hall! “I truly hope it’s the person who I suspect. If it is, things are going to get interesting.”

With that, Sir Star Ring stood and began walking away.

When Zhou Zhengli realized he was planning to leave, he said, “Exalted one, how are you going to respond to all this?”

Sir Star Ring didn’t bother looking back. As he walked out of the hall, he said, “I’d originally been planning to throw some threats around to certain people. This just gives me the perfect reason to do so. By the way, you don’t need to constantly try to feign weakness. You know full well what you should be doing in this situation. It’s time for you to go handle the matter I assigned to you before.”[1]

With that, Sir Star Ring vanished.

Zhou Zhengli’s only reaction was a very faint smile. Rumors amount to covert plotting. And the only way to deal with covert plotting is with overt plotting. Unfortunately, considering I’m working with someone so outstanding, I have no choice but to feign weakness, do I?[2]

***

It was midday.

Sir Star Ring materialized outside of the sword furnace and coolly said, “Someone got antsy, so tonight, I’m expelling them as an example.”

He spoke with calm confidence, and didn’t even bother waiting to see how Hordeslayer and Rampart would react before leaving.

When he reappeared, he was in the university’s secluded meditation facilities, where Li the Chosen was located. He said exactly the same thing in exactly the same tone.

Next, he arrived at the guest hall. He and Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix did not meet in person. He just stood outside and said the same thing. He did not speak the words out loud, but instead, said them directly into her mind. Even as she stirred in shock, Fourth True Monarch disappeared.

He didn’t just visit them. An instant later, he materialized in front of Li Mengtu, who was on his way to Young Aurora Hall in the guise of Zhong Chi.

Li Mengtu’s heart sank, but he made sure to keep a respectful expression on his face. As he bowed in greeting, Fourth True Monarch said the same words as before. Then he continued on to other locations.

It didn’t take long for him to visit all of the people he was certain were outsiders. All of them could sense the somber nature of the words he spoke to them. He was telling them very clearly what he was going to do. And it would happen that very night!

Midday passed and the sun set. Everything seemed peaceful and calm, but there were undercurrents. Eventually, night fell. Stars twinkled in the sky as the moon slowly rose and cast out gentle, silvery light. It was like gauze that covered the entire immortal palace. The darkness of night added something mysterious to the palace, making the people seem like mirages in a dream. In those mirages, immortal music drifted and immortal fairies danced gracefully.

Hordeslayer and Rampart were completely on guard in the sword furnace. Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix waited in combat readiness in the guest hall. Li Mengtu had not yet gone back into Young Aurora Hall. He was waiting outside.

The night became deep. The bright moonlight glittered on the lavish decorations in the palace, making them glitter like stars....

***

In an office in the Scourgebolt Palace, which managed the Scourgebolt Cliffs, one of the corrections officers opened his eyes.

He was a middle-age man with a resolute expression on his face. He was currently standing and fiddling with a jade slip. The jade slip contained an operations diagram of the immortal palace. It explained all the deployments and duty shifts, information from the spell formations, and most importantly, it explained what the highest ranking true monarchs were doing. The corrections officer looked at the jade slip, and his eyes glittered.

Selling this information will constitute a betrayal of the immortal palace, and it will definitely create waves. And the waves from a betrayal like that will be more than enough to satisfy the broken sword within me.

1. What I’m rendering as ‘feign weakness’ actually has a slightly different dictionary definition. It took me a while, but I eventually realized that the author is not using it in the way it’s defined in the dictionary. It really caused a lot of trouble for me as I struggled to justify the dictionary definition with the way it’s used with Zhou Zhengli. In the end, I talked it over with Madam Deathblade and decided to render the term as ‘feign weakness.’ The reason, as you can see here and as will become more obvious in coming chapters, Zhou Zhengli is putting on a show of humility and ineptitude as a tactic to get what he wants. Unfortunately, this is actually the exact opposite of the dictionary definition of the term. In dictionaries (both in English and Chinese), the definition term is defined as: “to hide your incompetence by remaining silent.” He is actually intentionally acting incompetent to try to hide his true strength/skill/intentions. Much later on, the author uses a different word to describe Zhou Zhengli, and it's basically the same word used to describe Seventh Peak traditions back in the day, i.e. deceptive, or "hiding/concealing (the truth about oneself)". This kind of thing is not important enough to talk with the author about. He is either intentionally or unintentionally using the word in a different way than its dictionary definition. He does this thing occasionally with other words, idioms, etc. By the way, the reason I’m putting this explanation here is A) because I think it’s interesting and B) I know there are people who occasionally check the Chinese or perhaps have read in Chinese, and might be curious about why I make the translation choices I do. I’m not including it as a way to solicit input or advice about other ways I could have translated the term. ☜

2. Although my translation is accurate, it lacks some of the nuance of the original Chinese. The term for plot/conspiracy in Chinese takes the character for stratagem/plan/scheme and adds the yin character to the front (from yin and yang). As I’m sure many of you know, when it comes to yin and yang, the yin side generally refers to things that are feminine, dark, soft, and hidden. So in Chinese, a plot/conspiracy is a “yin stratagem” or perhaps you could say a “hidden stratagem.” Well, there’s also a common term that adds the yang character instead of the yin one. So in that case, it’s a “yang stratagem” or perhaps you could say an “open/overt stratagem.” Both terms are used here, and I’m rendering them as covert plotting and overt plotting to try to maintain a little bit of the wordplay element that you have in Chinese. ☜
